void bfs(PII start)
{
    queue<PII> q;

            if(a[x][y] =3D=3D '#') continue=
;//=E5=A6=82=E6=9E=9C=E6=98=AF'#',=E4=B8=8D=E5=

=9E=9C=E6=98=AF'E'=EF=BC=8C=E6=89=BE=E5=88=B0=E4=BA=86=EF=BC=8C=E8=BE=93=E5=

    }
    cout << "oop!" << endl;//=E6=B2=A1=E6=9C=89=E6=89=BE=E5=88=B0

}

int main()
{

    while(t--)
    {
